              * * *  Maple Integration Test Results - 2011-06-08  * * *


Test file:  RationalFunctions/RationalFunctionsOfLinears.txt

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = (a+b*x)^2/x^4
  Optimal integral = -1/3*(a+b*x)^3/a/x^3
  Maple integral   = -b^2/x-1/3*a^2/x^3-a*b/x^2
  Leafcounts = 17 26   17 26

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = x*(a+b*x)^3
  Optimal integral = -1/20*(a+b*x)^4*(a-4*b*x)/b^2
  Maple integral   = 1/5*b^3*x^5+3/4*a*b^2*x^4+a^2*b*x^3+1/2*a^3*x^2
  Leafcounts = 20 40   20 40

  Leafcounts = 17 39   17 39

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = (b+2*c*x+3*d*x^2)*(b*x+c*x^2+d*x^3)^7

  Integrand        = (b+2*c*x+3*d*x^2)*x^7*(b+c*x+d*x^2)^7

Valid but unnecessarily complicated antiderivative:
  Integrand        = (b+3*d*x^2)*(a+b*x+d*x^3)^7
